## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes ConfigMap Immutability Feature Migration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the ConfigMap and Secret immutability feature: the Immutable field validation, the mutation prevention logic, and the watch optimization that skips immutable objects.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [

  ],

  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

### 2. Immutable Field Validation & Mutation Prevention (API Server)

| File | Key Symbols | Role |
|---|---|---|
| `pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go` | `ValidateSecretUpdate`, `ValidateConfigMapUpdate` | Core enforcement: if `old.Immutable == true`, rejects any change to `data`/`binaryData` and rejects clearing the `Immutable` flag |
| `pkg/registry/core/secret/strategy.go` | `ValidateUpdate` | REST strategy for Secrets; calls `ValidateSecretUpdate` on every PUT/PATCH |
| `pkg/registry/core/configmap/strategy.go` | `ValidateUpdate` | REST strategy for ConfigMaps; calls `ValidateConfigMapUpdate` on every PUT/PATCH |

**Mutation-prevention call chain:**
```
API PUT/PATCH
  → strategy.ValidateUpdate()          (pkg/registry/core/{secret,configmap}/strategy.go)
    → validation.ValidateSecretUpdate() (pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go)
         checks: if oldSecret.Immutable == true
           → reject data changes (ValidateImmutableField)
           → reject clearing Immutable flag
```

## Summary: ConfigMap & Secret Immutability in kubernetes/kubernetes v1.32.0

The feature is implemented across **18 Go source files** spanning three distinct subsystems:

### Pillar 1 — Type Definitions (`Immutable *bool` field)
- `pkg/apis/core/types.go` — internal API structs for `Secret` and `ConfigMap`
- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go` — public v1 API structs

### Pillar 2 — Mutation Prevention (API Server)
- `pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go` — `ValidateSecretUpdate` / `ValidateConfigMapUpdate`: if the old object had `Immutable=true`, rejects any change to `data`/`binaryData` and rejects clearing the `Immutable` flag
- `pkg/registry/core/secret/strategy.go` — `ValidateUpdate` calls `ValidateSecretUpdate`
- `pkg/registry/core/configmap/strategy.go` — `ValidateUpdate` calls `ValidateConfigMapUpdate`
- `pkg/apis/core/validation/validation_test.go` — unit tests for both update validators

### Pillar 3 — Watch Optimization (Kubelet)
- `pkg/kubelet/util/manager/watch_based_manager.go` — defines `isImmutableFunc` type; `objectCacheItem` carries an `immutable bool`; `objectCache.Get()` calls `c.isImmutable(object)` and if true calls `item.setImmutable()` + `item.stop()` to permanently kill the reflector/watch; `restartReflectorIfNeeded()` skips restart for immutable items
- `pkg/kubelet/configmap/configmap_manager.go` — `NewWatchingConfigMapManager` defines `isImmutable = configMap.Immutable != nil && *configMap.Immutable`
- `pkg/kubelet/secret/secret_manager.go` — `NewWatchingSecretManager` defines the same closure for Secrets
- `pkg/kubelet/util/manager/watch_based_manager_test.go`
